routes</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_250" title="Puerto Rico Highway 250"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Ellipse_sign_250.svg/31px-Ellipse_sign_250.svg.png" decoding="async" width="31" height="25" class="mw-file-element" href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_252" title="Puerto Rico Highway 252"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Ellipse_sign_252.svg/31px-Ellipse_sign_252.svg.png" decoding="async" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Ellipse_sign_252.svg/62px-Ellipse_sign_252.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="240" data-file-height="192" /></a></span> <span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_253" title="Puerto Rico Highway 253"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Ellipse_sign_253.svg/31px-Ellipse_sign_253.svg.png" decoding="async" width="31" height="25" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Ellipse_sign_253.svg/47px-Ellipse_sign_253.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Ellipse_sign_253.svg/62px-Ellipse_sign_253.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="240" data-file-height="192" /></a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Isla Culebra</b> (<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1177148991">.mw-parser-output .IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">Spanish pronunciation:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="es-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">&#91;ku\xcb\x88le\xce\xb2\xc9\xbea&#93;</a></span>, <i>Snake Island</i>) is an island, <a href="/wiki/Culebra_barrio-pueblo" title="Culebra barrio-pueblo">town</a> and <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Municipalities of Puerto Rico">municipality</a> of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>, and together with <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a>, it is geographically part of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Virgin_Islands" title="Spanish Virgin Islands">Spanish Virgin Islands</a>. It is located approximately 17 miles (27&#160;km) east of the Puerto Rican mainland, 12 miles (19&#160;km) west of <a href="/wiki/Saint_Thomas,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Thomas, U.S. Virgin Islands">St. Thomas</a> and 9 miles (14&#160;km) north of <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a>. Culebra is spread over 5 barrios and <a href="/wiki/Culebra_Town" class="mw-redirect" title="Culebra Town">Culebra Pueblo (Dewey)</a>, the main town and the administrative center of the island. Residents of the island are known as c<i>ulebrenses</i>. With a population of 1,792 as of the 2020 Census, it is Puerto Rico\'s least populous municipality.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Originally called <i>Isla del Pasaje</i> and <i>Isla de San Ildefonso</i>, Culebra is also known as <i>Isla Chiquita</i> ("Little Island"), <i>Cuna del Sol Borincano</i> ("Cradle of the Puerto Rican Sun") and <i>\xc3\x9altima Virgen</i> ("Last Virgin", due to its position at the end of the <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Islands" title="Virgin Islands">Virgin Islands</a> archipelago).\n</p>\n<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Some sources claim that <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Columbus" title="Christopher Columbus">Christopher Columbus</a> was the first European to arrive at the island during his <a href="/wiki/Second_voyage_of_Christopher_Columbus" class="mw-redirect" title="Second voyage of Christopher Columbus">second voyage</a> on November 19, 1493.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Isla_de_Culebra_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Isla_de_Culebra-6"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> It is believed that the island was populated by <a href="/wiki/Island_Caribs" class="mw-redirect" title="Island Caribs">Carib Indians</a> during the <a href="/wiki/European_colonization_of_the_Americas" title="European colonization of the Americas">colonization</a>. After <a href="/wiki/Ag%C3%BCeyban%C3%A1_II" title="Ag\xc3\xbceyban\xc3\xa1 II">Ag\xc3\xbceyban\xc3\xa1 and Ag\xc3\xbceyban\xc3\xa1 II</a> led the <a href="/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_rebellion_of_1511" class="mw-redirect" title="Ta\xc3\xadno rebellion of 1511">Ta\xc3\xadno rebellion of 1511</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Ta\xc3\xadno people">Ta\xc3\xadno Indians</a> from the main island sought refuge on Culebra and allied with Caribs to launch random attacks at the island estates.<sup id="cite_ref-Historia_de_Culebra_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Historia_de_Culebra-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>After that, the island was left abandoned for centuries. During the era of Spanish commerce through the Americas, it was used as a refuge for <a href="/wiki/Pirate" class="mw-redirect" title="Pirate">pirates</a>, as well as local fishermen and sailors.<sup id="cite_ref-Historia_de_Culebra_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Historia_de_Culebra-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Some sources mention a black overseer from British-ruled <a href="/wiki/Tortola" title="Tortola">Tortola</a> named John Stevens, who was put in charge of Culebra in the 1850s by the Governor of Vieques under the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_crown" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish crown">Spanish crown</a> to protect the island from foreigners who, without proper permissions or payments of fees for despoiling Culebra, took fish, cut trees for lumber and prepared drift wood as charcoal for future sale elsewhere.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Appropriating the unearned title of "Captain", he began a decades-long isolated sojourn on Culebra as enforcer of Spanish interests. In October 1871, however, Stevens was found dead outside his hut, his body viciously hacked apart. His heart and entrails had been placed in clay pots, in an apparent religious ritual to curse his soul. Spanish police from Vieques tracked down <a href="/wiki/Tortola" title="Tortola">Tortolan</a> foragers on Culebra who were suspected of the vicious murder. Eventually 21 of them were sentenced to forced labor on sugar plantations in <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a> as punishment. The affair caused an international incident, and, to satisfy demands from the <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British</a> ambassador in <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a>, the Tortolans were finally freed by the Spanish Governor of Puerto Rico in July 1874.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> \nThese events caused the government of <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> in June 1876 to recall an expedition destined for Culebra to establish a warm-weather sanatorium there. Fearing further foreign encroachments, the Spanish government decided to populate Culebra with its own subjects.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Culebra was then settled by Cayetano Escudero Sanz on October 27, 1880, when he completed his survey of the island that included subdivisions into usable lots. The Spanish government offered these parcels of land to anyone who would move to the island. The first settlers depended on rain for drinking water, as the island has no natural streams. <a href="/wiki/Subsistence_farming" class="mw-redirect" title="Subsistence farming">Subsistence farming</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cattle_raising" class="mw-redirect" title="Cattle raising">cattle raising</a> were established and a cistern was built for common use at one end of a natural harbor or <i>Ensenada Honda</i> in Spanish.\n</p><p>This first settlement was called <b>San Ildefonso</b>, to honor the Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Toledo,_Spain" title="Toledo, Spain">Toledo</a>, officially <b>San Ildefonso de la Culebra</b>. Two years later, on September 25, 1882, construction of the <a href="/wiki/Culebrita" class="mw-redirect" title="Culebrita">Culebrita</a> <a href="/wiki/Culebrita_Lighthouse" title="Culebrita Lighthouse">lighthouse</a> began. It was completed on February 25, 1886, which made it the oldest operating lighthouse in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a> until 1975, when the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">U.S. Navy</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">Coast Guard</a> finally closed the facility.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Puerto Rico was ceded by <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> in the aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish%E2%80%93American_War" title="Spanish\xe2\x80\x93American War">Spanish\xe2\x80\x93American War</a> under the terms of the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Paris_of_1898" class="mw-redirect" title="Treaty of Paris of 1898">Treaty of Paris of 1898</a> and became a territory of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. In 1899, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_War" title="United States Department of War">United States Department of War</a> conducted a <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">census</a> of Puerto Rico finding that the population of Culebra was 704.<sup id="cite_ref-OfficeSanger1900_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OfficeSanger1900-12"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In 1902, Culebra was integrated as a part of <a href="/wiki/Vieques" class="mw-redirect" title="Vieques">Vieques</a>. One year later, on June 26, <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">President Theodore Roosevelt</a> established the Culebra Naval Reservation. A bird refuge was established on February 27, 1909.<sup id="cite_ref-Isla_de_Culebra_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Isla_de_Culebra-6"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Historia_de_Culebra_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Historia_de_Culebra-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> cited the 1900 <a href="/wiki/Foraker_Act" title="Foraker Act">Foraker Act</a> to expropriate the land surrounding the natural harbor and in 1902 ordered the removal of all settlers so that a base for the South Atlantic fleet could be erected. Antonio Lugo Suarez, a Puerto Rican who had made his fortune in <a href="/wiki/Saint_Thomas,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint Thomas, U.S. Virgin Islands">St. Thomas</a> then part of the <a href="/wiki/Danish_West_Indies" title="Danish West Indies">Danish West Indies</a> and Pedro M\xc3\xa1rquez Morales, a <a href="/wiki/Spaniards" title="Spaniards">Spaniard</a> who had married a <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Ricans" title="Puerto Ricans">Puerto Rican</a> woman from Vieques, were successful ranchers on Culebra. Each offered an alternate site to the displaced Culebrenses, so as to prevent the total abandonment of the island. The location identified by M\xc3\xa1rquez on Playa Sardinas became the town of <b><a href="/wiki/Culebra_barrio-pueblo" title="Culebra barrio-pueblo">Dewey</a></b>.<sup id="cite_ref-NYT_2014_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYT_2014-13"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>A new church was built with materials taken from San Ildefonso and a customs office was constructed.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\nPedro M\xc3\xa1rquez (1850\xe2\x80\x931920) was appointed the first mayor under U.S. rule in 1905, replacing Leopoldo Padr\xc3\xb3n, the Special Delegate appointed for the transition from Spanish rule. \nPedro M\xc3\xa1rquez was succeeded as mayor in 1912 by his son, Alejandro M\xc3\xa1rquez Laureano (1912\xe2\x80\x931914) who erected the first docks for the new town and installed electric lighting on the town\'s streets. He was succeeded as mayor in 1914 by Claro C. Feliciano, the first mayor who had been born in Culebra.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>With the agreement reached with a new <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuban</a> government to lease <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_Naval_Base" title="Guantanamo Bay Naval Base">Guantanamo Bay</a> as a naval base, in 1911 the U.S. reduced the size of its forces on Culebra and turned the installation to training purposes.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> In 1924, the U.S. Navy began annual maneuvers on Culebra taking advantage of its deep-sea waters to practice coordinating amphibious landings on its beaches.\n</p><p>In 1939, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">U.S. Navy</a> began to use the Culebra Archipelago as a gunnery and bombing practice site. This was done in preparation for the United States\' involvement in <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. In 1971 the people of Culebra began protests, known as the <a href="/wiki/Navy-Culebra_protests" class="mw-redirect" title="Navy-Culebra protests">Navy-Culebra protests</a>, for the removal of the U.S. Navy from Culebra. Four years later, in 1975, the use of Culebra as a gunnery range ceased and all operations were moved to <a href="/wiki/Vieques" class="mw-redirect" title="Vieques">Vieques</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Culebra was declared an independent island municipality in 1917. The first democratically elected government was put into place in 1960. Prior to this, the government of Puerto Rico appointed delegates to administer the island.\n</p><p>On September 20, 2017, <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">Hurricane Maria</a> struck the island of Puerto Rico.  In Culebra, where <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">Hurricane Irma</a> had caused major damages a week prior, Hurricane Maria caused more destruction.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Geography">Geography</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg/250px-Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="205" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg/375px-Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg/500px-Culebra_Nautical_chart.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4565" data-file-height="3750" /></a><figcaption>Culebra nautical chart</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Culebra is an <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelago</a> consisting of the main island and twenty-three smaller islands that lie off its coast. The largest of these <a href="/wiki/Cay" title="Cay">keys</a> are: <a href="/wiki/Culebrita" class="mw-redirect" title="Culebrita">Culebrita</a> to the east, <a href="/wiki/Cayo_Norte" title="Cayo Norte">Cayo Norte</a> to the northeast, and <a href="/wiki/Cayo_Luis_Pe%C3%B1a" title="Cayo Luis Pe\xc3\xb1a">Cayo Luis Pe\xc3\xb1a</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayo_Lobo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cayo Lobo (page does not exist)">Cayo Lobo</a> to the west. The smaller islands include Cayo Ballena, Cayos Geniqui, Arrecife Culebrita, Las Hermanas, El Mono, Cayo Lobito, Cayo Botijuela, Alcarraza, Los Gemelos, and Piedra Steven. Islands in the archipelago are <a href="/wiki/Arid" class="mw-redirect" title="Arid">arid</a>, meaning they have no rivers or <a href="/wiki/Stream" title="Stream">streams</a>. All of the <a href="/wiki/Fresh_water" title="Fresh water">fresh water</a> is brought from Puerto Rico via Vieques by undersea pipeline.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-20"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Culebra is characterized by an irregular <a href="/wiki/Topography" title="Topography">topography</a> resulting in a long intricate <a href="/wiki/Coast" title="Coast">shoreline</a>. The island is approximately 7 by 5 miles (11 by 8&#160;km). The coast is marked by cliffs, sandy coral <a href="/wiki/Beach" title="Beach">beaches</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mangrove" title="Mangrove">mangrove</a> <a href="/wiki/Forest" title="Forest">forests</a>. Inland, the tallest point on the island is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mount_Resaca&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mount Resaca (page does not exist)">Mount Resaca</a>, with an elevation of 636 feet (193.9 meters),<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> followed by Balc\xc3\xb3n Hill, with an elevation of 545 feet (166.1 meters).<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ensenada_Honda_(Culebra,_Puerto_Rico)" title="Ensenada Honda (Culebra, Puerto Rico)">Ensenada Honda</a> is the largest inlet on the island and is considered to be the most <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">hurricane</a> secure harbor in the Caribbean.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan-23"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> There are also several <a href="/wiki/Lagoon" title="Lagoon">lagoons</a> on the island, like Corcho, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Flamenco_Lagoon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Flamenco Lagoon (page does not exist)">Flamenco</a>, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Zoni_Lagoon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Zoni Lagoon (page does not exist)">Zon\xc3\xad</a>. Culebrita Island also has a lagoon called Molino.\n</p><p>Almost 80% of the island\'s area is <a href="/wiki/Volcanic" class="mw-redirect" title="Volcanic">volcanic</a> rock from the <a href="/wiki/Cretaceous" title="Cretaceous">Cretaceous</a> period. It is mostly used for <a href="/wiki/Livestock" title="Livestock">livestock</a> pasture, as well as some minor <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">agriculture</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Average_sea_temperature">Average sea temperature</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Average sea temperature"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div>\n<table class="wikitable mw-collapsible" style="width:auto; text-align:center; line-height:1.2em;">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="14">Climate data for Average sea temperature\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Month\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Jan\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Feb\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Mar\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Apr\n</th>\n<th scope="col">May\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Jun\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Jul\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Aug\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Sep\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Oct\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Nov\n</th>\n<th scope="col">Dec\n</th>\n<th scope="col" style="border-left-width:medium">Year\n</th></tr>\n<tr style="text-align: center;">\n<th scope="row" style="height: 16px;">Daily mean \xc2\xb0F (\xc2\xb0C)\n</th>\n<td style="background: #FF6900; color:#000000;" class="notheme">79.2<br />(26.2)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF6C00; color:#000000;" class="notheme">78.3<br />(25.7)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF6C00; color:#000000;" class="notheme">78.4<br />(25.8)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF6600; color:#000000;" class="notheme">80.1<br />(26.7)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF6100; color:#000000;" class="notheme">81.1<br />(27.3)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5C00; color:#000000;" class="notheme">82.6<br />(28.1)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5A00; color:#000000;" class="notheme">83.1<br />(28.4)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5600; color:#000000;" class="notheme">84.2<br />(29.0)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5400; color:#000000;" class="notheme">84.7<br />(29.3)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5600; color:#000000;" class="notheme">84.2<br />(29.0)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5A00; color:#000000;" class="notheme">83.1<br />(28.4)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF6100; color:#000000;" class="notheme">81.3<br />(27.4)\n</td>\n<td style="background: #FF5F00; color:#000000; border-left-width:medium" class="notheme">81.7<br />(27.6)\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="14" style="text-align:center;font-size:95%;">Source: SeaTemperatures.org <sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Federal_nature_reserves">Federal nature reserves</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Federal nature reserves"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG/250px-Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG/375px-Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG/500px-Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge_Map.JPG 2x" data-file-width="539" data-file-height="406" /></a><figcaption>Map of the Culebra National Wildlife Refuge</figcaption></figure>\n<p>These small islands are all classified as nature reserves and several nature reserves also exist on the main island. One of the oldest bird sanctuaries in United States territory was established in Culebra on February 27, 1909, by President <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Teddy Roosevelt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Flora_and_Fauna_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flora_and_Fauna-26"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Culebra_Island_giant_anole" class="mw-redirect" title="Culebra Island giant anole">Culebra Island giant anole</a> (<i>Anolis roosevelti</i>, <i>Xiphosurus roosevelti</i> (according to ITIS) is an extremely rare or possibly extinct <a href="/wiki/Anole_lizard" class="mw-redirect" title="Anole lizard">anole lizard</a>. It is native to Culebra Island and was named in honor of <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt_Jr." title="Theodore Roosevelt Jr.">Theodore Roosevelt Jr.</a>, who was the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Governor of Puerto Rico">governor of Puerto Rico</a> at that time. There are bird sanctuaries on many of the islands as well as <a href="/wiki/Sea_turtle" title="Sea turtle">turtle</a> nesting sites on Culebra. <a href="/wiki/Leatherback_sea_turtle" title="Leatherback sea turtle">Leatherback</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green_sea_turtle" title="Green sea turtle">green sea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hawksbill_turtle" class="mw-redirect" title="Hawksbill turtle">hawksbill</a> <a href="/wiki/Sea_turtle" title="Sea turtle">sea turtles</a> use the beaches for nesting. The archipelagos bird sanctuaries are home to <a href="/wiki/Brown_booby" title="Brown booby">brown boobies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Laughing_gull" title="Laughing gull">laughing gulls</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sooty_tern" title="Sooty tern">sooty terns</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bridled_tern" title="Bridled tern">bridled terns</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tern" title="Tern">noddy terns</a>. An estimated 50,000 <a href="/wiki/Seabird" title="Seabird">seabirds</a> find their way back to the sanctuaries every year. These nature reserves comprise 1,568 acres (635&#160;ha) of the <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">archipelago</a>\'s 7,000 acres (2,800&#160;ha). These nature reserves are protected by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Fish_and_Wildlife_Service" title="United States Fish and Wildlife Service">United States Fish and Wildlife Service</a>.\n</p><p>Culebra has no natural large mammals. However, a population of <a href="/wiki/White-tailed_deer" title="White-tailed deer">white-tailed deer</a> introduced in July 1966 (one male and three females) can be found on the eastern region of the island.<sup id="cite_ref-Flora_and_Fauna_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Flora_and_Fauna-26"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="National_protected_area">National protected area</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: National protected area"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Culebra_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Culebra National Wildlife Refuge">Culebra National Wildlife Refuge</a></li></ul>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png/250px-Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="152" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png/375px-Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png/500px-Isla_Culebra_barrios_ES.png 2x" data-file-width="933" data-file-height="567" /></a><figcaption>Culebra with barrios</figcaption></figure>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Important_Bird_Area">Important Bird Area</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Important Bird Area"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Culebra, along with its adjacent islets and cays, has been recognised as an <a href="/wiki/Important_Bird_Area" title="Important Bird Area">Important Bird Area</a> (IBA) by <a href="/wiki/BirdLife_International" title="BirdLife International">BirdLife International</a> because they support <a href="/wiki/Seabird" title="Seabird">seabird</a> <a href="/wiki/Bird_colony" title="Bird colony">breeding colonies</a> of <a href="/wiki/Brown_booby" title="Brown booby">brown boobies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brown_noddy" title="Brown noddy">brown noddies</a>, and both <a href="/wiki/Sooty_tern" title="Sooty tern">sooty</a> and <a href="/wiki/Royal_tern" title="Royal tern">royal terns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-bli_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bli-27"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Barrios">Barrios</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Barrios"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Like all municipalities of Puerto Rico, Culebra is subdivided into <a href="/wiki/Barrios_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Barrios of Puerto Rico">barrios</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pico_1969_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pico_1969-28"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Law2015_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Law2015-29"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-US2010Census_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-US2010Census-30"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<th><i>Barrio</i></th>\n<th>Area<br /><a href="/wiki/Square_metre" title="Square class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Sectors">Sectors</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Sectors"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_barrios_and_sectors_of_Culebra,_Puerto_Rico" title="List of barrios and sectors of Culebra, Puerto Rico">List of barrios and sectors of Culebra, Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Barrios (which are, in contemporary times, roughly comparable to <a href="/wiki/Minor_civil_divisions" class="mw-redirect" title="Minor civil divisions">minor civil divisions</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-Barrio-Pueblo_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barrio-Pueblo-33"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> are further subdivided into smaller areas called <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">sectores</i></span>  (<i>sectors</i> in English).  The types of <i>sectores</i> may vary, from normally <i>sector</i> to <i>urbanizaci\xc3\xb3n</i> to <i>reparto</i> to <i>barriada</i> to <i>residencial</i>, among others.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Law_1-2001_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Law_1-2001-36"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Tourism">Tourism</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Tourism"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Playa_Flamenco_(15584144756).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg/220px-Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg/330px-Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg/440px-Playa_Flamenco_%2815584144756%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="3456" /></a><figcaption>Flamenco Beach</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Culebra is a popular weekend tourist destination for mainland <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Ricans</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">Americans</a> and residents of <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a>.\nCulebra has many beaches including <a href="/wiki/Flamenco_Beach" title="Flamenco Beach">Flamenco Beach</a> (<i>Playa Flamenco</i>), rated third best beach in the world for 2014 by <a href="/wiki/TripAdvisor" class="mw-redirect" title="TripAdvisor">TripAdvisor</a>. In November 2017 Forbes rated it #19 of the top 50 beaches around the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Forbes_19_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Forbes_19-37"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> It can be reached by shuttle buses from the ferry. The beach extends for a mile of white coral sand and is framed beautifully by arid tree-covered hills. The beach is also protected by the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Department_of_Natural_and_Environmental_Resources" title="Puerto Rico Department of Natural and Environmental Resources">Department of Natural and Environmental Resources</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Marine_reserve" title="Marine reserve">marine wildlife reserve</a>.\n</p><p>The area west of Flamenco Beach and the adjacent Flamenco Point were used for joint-<a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a>/<a href="/wiki/United_States_Marine_Corps" title="United States Marine Corps">Marine Corps</a> military exercises until 1975. Two old <a href="/wiki/M4_Sherman" title="M4 Sherman">M4 Sherman</a> tanks, which were used for target practice, can be found at the beach. Culebra and <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a> offered the U.S. military training areas for the <a href="/wiki/Fleet_Marine_Force" title="Fleet Marine Force">Fleet Marine Force</a> in <a href="/wiki/Amphibious_warfare" title="Amphibious warfare">amphibious</a> exercises for <a href="/wiki/Beachhead" title="Beachhead">beach landings</a> and <a href="/wiki/Naval_gunfire_support" title="Naval gunfire support">naval gunfire support</a> testing. Culebra and Vieques were the two components of the Atlantic Fleet Weapons Range Inner Range. In recent years, only the shortened term "Inner Range" was used.\n</p>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg/220px-Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="140" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg/330px-Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg/440px-Underwater_corals_on_the_Island_of_Culebra.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="1146" /></a><figcaption>Coral reef on Culebra</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Other beaches are only accessible by private car or boats. Of the smaller islands, only <a href="/wiki/Culebrita" class="mw-redirect" title="Culebrita">Culebrita</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cayo_Luis_Pe%C3%B1a" title="Cayo Luis Pe\xc3\xb1a">Luis Pe\xc3\xb1a</a> permit visitors and can be accessible via water taxis from Culebra. Hiking and nature photography are encouraged on the small islands. However, activities which would disturb the nature reserves are prohibited, e.g. <a href="/wiki/Camping" title="Camping">camping</a>, <a href="/wiki/Litter" title="Litter">littering</a> and the use of <a href="/wiki/Automobile" class="mw-redirect" title="Automobile">motor vehicles</a>. Camping, however, is allowed on Flamenco Beach throughout the year. Reservations are recommended.<sup id="cite_ref-Camping_Culebra_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Camping_Culebra-38"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\nCulebra is also a popular destination for <a href="/wiki/Scuba_set" title="Scuba set">scuba divers</a> because of the many reefs throughout the archipelago and the crystal clear waters. Because of the "arid" nature of the island there is no run-off from rivers or streams, resulting in very clear waters around the archipelago.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Landmarks_and_places_of_interest">Landmarks and places of interest</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Landmarks and places of interest"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>To stimulate local tourism, the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Tourism_Company" title="Puerto Rico Tourism Company">Puerto Rico Tourism Company</a> launched the <i>Voy Turistiendo</i> ("I\'m Touring") campaign, with a passport book and website. The Culebra page lists <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Playa Flamenco</i></span>, <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Faro de Culebrita</i></span>, and <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Reserva Natural del Canal Luis Pe\xc3\xb1a</i></span>, as places of interest.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>39<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Culebra_museum.JPG" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Culebra_museum.JPG/200px-Culebra_museum.JPG" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Culebra_museum.JPG/300px-Culebra_museum.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Culebra_museum.JPG/400px-Culebra_museum.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2304" data-file-height="1728" /></a><figcaption>U. S. Navy ammunitions warehouse built in 1905. It is now Culebra\'s Historical Museum.</figcaption></figure>\n<p>According to a news article by <a href="/wiki/Primera_Hora_(Puerto_Rico)" title="Primera Hora (Puerto Rico)">Primera Hora</a>, Culebra has 10 beaches.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Flamenco_Beach" title="Flamenco Beach">Flamenco Beach</a> (Ranked #2 in the top 10 most exotic beaches in the world)<sup id="cite_ref-Beach_Bum_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Beach_Bum-41"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>41<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>42<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Brava Beach</li>\n<li>Las Vacas Beach</li>\n<li>Larga Beach</li>\n<li>Pueblo Espa\xc3\xb1ol</li>\n<li>Punta Soldado Beach<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>43<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Resaca Beach</li>\n<li>Tamarindo Beach</li>\n<li>Tortuga Beach</li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Zon%C3%AD_Beach&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Zon\xc3\xad Beach (page does not exist)">Zon\xc3\xad Beach</a></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Culture">Culture</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Culture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Festivals_and_events">Festivals and events</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Festivals and events"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Culebra celebrates its <a href="/wiki/Fiestas_patronales_in_Puerto_Rico" title="Fiestas patronales in Puerto Rico">patron saint</a> festival in July. The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Fiestas Patronales de Nuestra Se\xc3\xb1ora del Carmen</i></span> is a religious and cultural celebration\nin honor of <a href="/wiki/Mary,_mother_of_Jesus" title="Mary, mother of Jesus">Mary, the mother of Jesus</a> and generally features parades, games, artisans, amusement rides, regional food, and live entertainment.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-20"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Other festivals and events include:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Windsurfing" title="Windsurfing">Windsurfing</a> competition \xe2\x80\x93 February</li>\n<li>Fishing tournament \xe2\x80\x93 March</li>\n<li>Craft festivities \xe2\x80\x93 November</li></ul>\n<p>In 2020, the descendants of Pedro M\xc3\xa1rquez erected a plaque commemorating the centennial of his death at the original site of his butcher shop, built on the main street that bears his name.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Economy">Economy</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Economy"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="thumb tnone" style="margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;overflow:hidden;width:auto;max-width:808px"><div class="thumbinner"><div class="noresize" style="overflow:auto"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg" class="mw-file-description" title="Culebra on the horizon as seen from Vieques"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg/800px-Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg" decoding="async" width="800" height="143" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg/1200px-Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3e/Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1394" data-file-height="250" /></a></span></div><div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ostrov_Culebra_panorama.jpg" title="File:Ostrov Culebra panorama.jpg"> </a></div>Culebra on the horizon as seen from <a href="/wiki/Vieques" class="mw-redirect" title="Vieques">Vieques</a></div></div></div>\n<p>In past centuries, <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">agriculture</a> was the main source of economy in Culebra. At some point, the following products were produced and <a href="/wiki/Exported" class="mw-redirect" title="Exported">exported</a> from the island: <a href="/wiki/Wood" title="Wood">wood</a>, turtle oil, shells, fish, <a href="/wiki/Tobacco" title="Tobacco">tobacco</a>, <a href="/wiki/Livestock" title="Livestock">livestock</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pig" title="Pig">pigs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goats" class="mw-redirect" title="Goats">goats</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cheese" title="Cheese">cheese</a>, <a href="/wiki/Plantain_(cooking)" class="mw-redirect" title="Plantain (cooking)">plantains</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pumpkin" title="Pumpkin">pumpkins</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bean" title="Bean">beans</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yam_(vegetable)" title="Yam (vegetable)">yams</a>, <a href="/wiki/Garlic" title="Garlic">garlic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maize" title="Maize">maize</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tomato" title="Tomato">tomatoes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Orange_(fruit)" title="Orange (fruit)">oranges</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coconut" title="Coconut">coconut</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cotton" title="Cotton">cotton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Melon" title="Melon">melons</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mangrove" title="Mangrove">mangrove</a> <a href="/wiki/Bark_(botany)" title="Bark (botany)">bark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coal" title="Coal">coal</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Domestic_turkey" title="Domestic turkey">turkey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Historia_-_Culebra_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Historia_-_Culebra-44"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>44<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Nowadays, Culebra\'s main source of revenue comes from <a href="/wiki/Construction" title="Construction">construction</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tourism" title="Tourism">tourism</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>45<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Demographics">Demographics</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Demographics"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1224496135">.mw-parser-output .us-census-pop{border-spacing:1px;border:1px solid class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></td></tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="2020">2020</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2020"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>As of 2020, the municipality has a population of 1,792, making it the least populous in Puerto Rico.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>53<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>10.8% of Culebra\'s population is of non-Hispanic origin, making it also the least Hispanic municipality in Puerto Rico. This represents an increase from 2010, when only 8.3% of the population was non-Hispanic.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>54<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Historic_demographics">Historic demographics</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Historic demographics"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In 1894, written reports indicated that there were 519 residents living in five communities: San Ildefonso, <a href="/wiki/Flamenco,_Culebra,_Puerto_Rico" title="Flamenco, Culebra, Puerto Rico">Flamenco</a>, San Isidero, Playa Sardinas I y II, and Frayle. There were 84 houses built, 24 of them in the San Ildefonso community.<sup id="cite_ref-Historia_-_Culebra_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Historia_-_Culebra-44"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>44<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notable_people_from_Culebra">Notable people from Culebra</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Notable people from Culebra"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pedro_Morales" title="Pedro Morales">Pedro Morales</a>, (1942\xe2\x80\x932019) was a Puerto Rican professional wrestler. The first Latino to hold a world heavyweight championship when he became the WWF <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a> World Heavyweight Champion in 1971.</li>\n<li><figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Avenida_Hermanos_Avila,_Culebra.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg/220px-Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg/330px-Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg/440px-Avenida_Hermanos_Avila%2C_Culebra.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3264" data-file-height="2448" /></a><figcaption>Avenida Hermanos \xc3\x81vila Esperanza - Puerto Rico Highway 251 (PR-251)</figcaption></figure><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.primerahora.com/noticias/puerto-rico/notas/orgullosos-de-ser-veteranos/">Hermanos \xc3\x81vila Esperanza</a> - Military (Andr\xc3\xa9s; Pedro; Norberto; Justino; Guillermo y Tom\xc3\xa1s) - A street in <a href="/wiki/Fajardo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Fajardo, Puerto Rico">Fajardo</a> (Parcelas Beltr\xc3\xa1n) and Culebra (<a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_251" title="Puerto Rico Highway 251">PR-251</a>) is named after The \xc3\x81vila Brothers. These six soldiers were honored for their exceptional work in the Korean and Vietnam wars and for returning home to Puerto Rico alive.</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Government">Government</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Government"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Culebra,_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG/250px-Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG/375px-Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG/500px-Culebra%2C_Puerto_Rico_City_Hall.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2304" data-file-height="1728" /></a><figcaption>Culebra\'s <a href="/wiki/City_hall" class="mw-redirect" title="City hall">city hall</a></figcaption></figure>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Mayoralty_in_Puerto_Rico" class="mw-redirect" title="Mayoralty in Puerto Rico">Mayoralty in Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Like all of Puerto Rico\'s municipalities, the island of Culebra is administered by a <a href="/wiki/Mayor" title="Mayor">mayor</a>, elected every four years in general elections. Initially, administrators were selected by the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_crown" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish crown">Spanish crown</a> or by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_government" class="mw-redirect" title="United States government">United States government</a> during the 19th and early 20th century.\n</p><p>In 2004, Abraham Pe\xc3\xb1a Nieves was elected mayor of Culebra with 50.1% of the votes.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> He was reelected in 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>56<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>In November 2011, Pe\xc3\xb1a died of <a href="/wiki/Prostate_cancer" title="Prostate cancer">prostate cancer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>57<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The next day, it was announced that his daughter, Lizaida Pe\xc3\xb1a, might replace him until the 2012 general elections.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> However, in 2011, <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_L%C3%B3pez_Cepero" title="Ricardo L\xc3\xb3pez Cepero">Ricardo L\xc3\xb3pez Cepero</a> was elected by delegates to succeed Pe\xc3\xb1a. L\xc3\xb3pez Cepero was defeated by <a href="/wiki/Iv%C3%A1n_Sol%C3%ADs" title="Iv\xc3\xa1n Sol\xc3\xads">Iv\xc3\xa1n Sol\xc3\xads</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_general_election,_2012" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rican general election, 2012">2012 general election</a>.\n</p><p>The city belongs to the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Senatorial_district_VIII" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Senatorial district VIII">Puerto Rico Senatorial district VIII</a>, which is represented by two senators. In 2012, <a href="/wiki/Pedro_A._Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Pedro A. Rodr\xc3\xadguez">Pedro A. Rodr\xc3\xadguez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luis_Daniel_Rivera" title="Luis Daniel Rivera">Luis Daniel Rivera</a> were elected as district senators.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>59<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Government_services">Government services</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Government services"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">United States Postal Service</a> operates the Culebra Post Office.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Symbols">Symbols</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Symbols"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">municipio</i></span> has an official flag and coat of arms.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>61<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Flag">Flag</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Flag"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The Culebra flag consists of five vertical stripes, three alternate yellow and two green ones. The yellow central stripe has the map of Culebra in green.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-62"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>62<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Coat of arms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The field is <i>tierced</i> in three, in the Spanish manner, <i>vert, argent, or</i>. The cross and the episcopal <a href="/wiki/Crozier" title="Crozier">crozier</a> symbolize Bishop San Ildefonso, because originally the island was called <b>San Ildefonso de la Culebra</b>. The crowned serpent (<i>culebra</i> means <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">serpent</a>) <i>ondoyant in pale</i> is the emblem of its name. The mailed arm refers to the coat of the Escudero family, first settlers of the island. The laurel cross refers to the civic triumph reached when Culebra obtained the evacuation of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a>. The crest is a coronet bearing two masts, their sails filled by the wind.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-62"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>62<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Education">Education</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Education"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Due to its size and small population, there are only three schools on Culebra, one for each level. They are the San Ildefonso Elementary School, the Antonio R. Barcel\xc3\xb3 High School, and the Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Rivera school. Education is administered by the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Department_of_Education" title="Puerto Rico Department of Education">Puerto Rico Department of Education</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Health_care">Health care</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Health care"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>There is a small hospital in the island called Hospital de Culebra. It also offers <a href="/wiki/Pharmacy" title="Pharmacy">pharmacy</a> services to residents and visitors. For emergencies, patients are transported by plane to <a href="/wiki/Fajardo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Fajardo, Puerto Rico">Fajardo</a> on the main island.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>63<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>On September 20, 2020, Puerto Rico\'s Health Department reported that in the six months of pandemic, Culebra had reported only six cases of infection and no deaths. This was the lowest rate of infection in any municipality of Puerto Rico during the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Puerto_Rico" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Puerto Rico">COVID-19 infections</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>64<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Transportation">Transportation</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Transportation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The island of Culebra can be reached by private boat, the <a href="/wiki/Culebra_Ferry" title="Culebra Ferry">Culebra Ferry</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Airplane" title="Airplane">airplane</a>. Ferry service is available from <a href="/wiki/Ceiba,_Puerto_Rico" title="Ceiba, Puerto Rico">Ceiba</a>. Ferries make several trips a day to the main island for an approximate fare of $4.50 (round trip).<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>66<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Culebra also has a small airport, <a href="/wiki/Benjam%C3%ADn_Rivera_Noriega_Airport" title="Benjam\xc3\xadn Rivera Noriega Airport">Benjam\xc3\xadn Rivera Noriega Airport</a>, with domestic service to the mainland and <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a>. The airport is served by small airlines:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Air_Flamenco" title="Air Flamenco">Air Flamenco</a> provides service from <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Luis_Ribas_Dominicci_Airport" title="Fernando Luis Ribas Dominicci Airport">Fernando Luis Ribas Dominicci Airport</a> in Isla Grande, <a href="/wiki/Luis_Mu%C3%B1oz_Mar%C3%ADn_International_Airport" title="Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport">Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Mar\xc3\xadn International Airport</a> in San Juan, and <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Aponte_de_la_Torre_Airport" title="Jos\xc3\xa9 Aponte de la Torre Airport">Jos\xc3\xa9 Aponte de la Torre Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ceiba,_Puerto_Rico" title="Ceiba, Puerto Rico">Ceiba</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Vieques_Air_Link" title="Vieques Air Link">Vieques Air Link</a> provides service to Culebra from <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a>, Vieques, Ceiba and, formerly, <a href="/wiki/Fajardo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Fajardo, Puerto Rico">Fajardo</a>.</li></ul>\n<p>There is <a href="/wiki/Public_transportation" class="mw-redirect" title="Public transportation">public transportation</a> available in the island, through public cars and taxis.\n</p><p>There is one bridge on the island.<sup id="cite_ref-bridge_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bridge-67"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Navy_Culebra_protests">Navy Culebra protests</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Navy Culebra protests"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Navy%E2%80%93Culebra_protests" title="Navy\xe2\x80\x93Culebra protests">Navy\xe2\x80\x93Culebra protests</a></div>\n<p>The <b>Navy\xe2\x80\x93Culebra protests</b> is the name given by <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> <a href="/wiki/Mass_media" title="Mass media">media</a> to a series of protests starting in 1971 on the island of Culebra, <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> use of the island.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The protests led to the U.S. Navy abandoning its facilities on Culebra.\n</p><p>The historical backdrop was that in 1902, three years after the U.S. invasion of Puerto Rico, Culebra was integrated as a part of <a href="/wiki/Vieques,_Puerto_Rico" title="Vieques, Puerto Rico">Vieques</a>. But on June 26, 1903, U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore Roosevelt</a> established the Culebra Naval Reservation in Culebra. The suitability of Culebra and its topography for the technical requirements of naval gunfire and aircraft weapons exercises was recognized in 1936, and the Government of the United States declared Culebra and its adjacent waters as the Culebra Naval Defensive Sea Area in 1941. This military defense area included all coastal waters from high-tide elevation to three miles off shore. The naval gunnery and aircraft weapons ranges at Culebra played a considerable role, along with other gunnery facilities near Guantanamo Bay in Cuba, in the combat readiness of Allied Naval Forces during the <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">Second World War</a>. These Caribbean ranges again served as primary weapons training grounds for both Naval Gunfire Support Exercises and aircraft weapons systems proficiency during the critical period of the Korean War starting in the summer of 1950. The United States Naval exercises reached a peak in 1969, as many ships and air units were attached to the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Fleet_(United_States)" class="mw-redirect" title="Atlantic Fleet (United States)">Atlantic Fleet</a> for gunnery and aerial ordnance proficiency prior to their ultimate assignments to naval task forces stationed in <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a>.\n</p><p>In 1971 the people of Culebra began the protests for the removal of the U.S. Navy from Culebra. The protests were led by <a href="/wiki/Ruben_Berrios" class="mw-redirect" title="Ruben Berrios">Ruben Berrios</a>, President of the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_Independence_Party" title="Puerto Rican Independence Party">Puerto Rican Independence Party</a> (PIP), a well-regarded attorney in international rights, President-Honorary of the <a href="/wiki/Socialist_International" title="Socialist International">Socialist International</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Law" title="Law">Law</a> professor at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Puerto_Rico" title="University of Puerto Rico">University of Puerto Rico</a>. An ecumenical chapel was built on <a href="/wiki/Flamenco_Beach" title="Flamenco Beach">Flamenco Beach</a>, in an action led by <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic</a> Bishop Antulio Parilla Bonilla, <a href="/wiki/Baptists_in_the_United_States" title="Baptists in the United States">Baptist</a> minister, Luis Rivera Pag\xc3\xa1n, and George Lakey of the <a href="/wiki/Quakers" title="Quakers">Quaker</a> Action Committee.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Berrios and other protesters <a href="/wiki/Squatting" title="Squatting">squatted</a> in Culebra for a few days. Some of them, including Berrios, were arrested and imprisoned for <a href="/wiki/Civil_disobedience" title="Civil disobedience">civil disobedience</a>. The official charge was trespassing on U.S. military territory. The protests led to the U.S. Navy discontinuing the use of Culebra as a gunnery range in 1975 and all of its operations were moved to Vieques. The case against the Navy was led by <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington</a> lawyer Richard Copaken as retained pro-bono by the people of Culebra island.\n</p><p>The cleaning process of the island has been slow. At the end of 2016, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Corps_of_Engineers" title="United States Army Corps of Engineers">United States Army Corps of Engineers</a> sent letters to the residents of Culebra citing active removal of undetonated explosive material still present on the island.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>70<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="In_popular_culture">In popular culture</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Culebra,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: In popular culture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul><li>Two British sailing ships, the brig HMS <i>Triton</i> and the merchantman <i>Topaz</i>, are wrecked by a hurricane and come to rest with their crews on Isla Culebra in the novel <i><a href="/wiki/Governor_Ramage_R.N." title="Governor Ramage R.N.">Governor Ramage R.N.</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Pope" title="Dudley Pope">Dudley Pope</a></li>\n<li>As the site of an alleged buried treasure, Culebra is featured in the 2018 <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> <a href="/wiki/Docudrama" title="Docudrama">docudrama</a> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Legend_of_Cocaine_Island" title="The Legend of Cocaine Island">The Legend of Cocaine Island</a></i>.</li></ul>\n<div
